\DoxyCodeLine{00031\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ SUPPORT\_DEFAULT\_FONT\ (default)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00032\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Default\ font\ is\ loaded\ on\ window\ initialization\ to\ be\ available\ for\ the\ user\ to\ render\ simple\ text.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00033\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ NOTE:\ If\ enabled,\ uses\ external\ module\ functions\ to\ load\ default\ raylib\ font\ (module:\ text)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00034\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00035\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ SUPPORT\_CAMERA\_SYSTEM}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00036\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Camera\ module\ is\ included\ (rcamera.h)\ and\ multiple\ predefined\ cameras\ are\ available:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00037\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ free,\ 1st/3rd\ person,\ orbital,\ custom}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00038\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00039\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ SUPPORT\_GESTURES\_SYSTEM}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00040\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Gestures\ module\ is\ included\ (rgestures.h)\ to\ support\ gestures\ detection:\ tap,\ hold,\ swipe,\ drag}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00041\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00042\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ SUPPORT\_MOUSE\_GESTURES}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00043\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Mouse\ gestures\ are\ directly\ mapped\ like\ touches\ and\ processed\ by\ gestures\ system.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00044\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00045\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ SUPPORT\_BUSY\_WAIT\_LOOP}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00046\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Use\ busy\ wait\ loop\ for\ timing\ sync,\ if\ not\ defined,\ a\ high-\/resolution\ timer\ is\ setup\ and\ used}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00047\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00048\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ SUPPORT\_PARTIALBUSY\_WAIT\_LOOP}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00049\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Use\ a\ partial-\/busy\ wait\ loop,\ in\ this\ case\ frame\ sleeps\ for\ most\ of\ the\ time\ and\ runs\ a\ busy-\/wait-\/loop\ at\ the\ end}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00050\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00051\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ SUPPORT\_SCREEN\_CAPTURE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00052\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Allow\ automatic\ screen\ capture\ of\ current\ screen\ pressing\ F12,\ defined\ in\ KeyCallback()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00053\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00054\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ SUPPORT\_GIF\_RECORDING}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00055\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Allow\ automatic\ gif\ recording\ of\ current\ screen\ pressing\ CTRL+F12,\ defined\ in\ KeyCallback()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00056\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00057\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ SUPPORT\_COMPRESSION\_API}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00058\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Support\ CompressData()\ and\ DecompressData()\ functions,\ those\ functions\ use\ zlib\ implementation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00059\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ provided\ by\ stb\_image\ and\ stb\_image\_write\ libraries,\ so,\ those\ libraries\ must\ be\ enabled\ on\ textures\ module}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00060\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ for\ linkage}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00061\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00062\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ SUPPORT\_AUTOMATION\_EVENTS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00063\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Support\ automatic\ events\ recording\ and\ playing,\ useful\ for\ automated\ testing\ systems\ or\ AI\ based\ game\ playing}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01235\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Compute\ aspect\ ratio}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01237\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01238\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Compute\ lens\ parameters}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01239\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ lensShift\ =\ (device.hScreenSize*0.25f\ -\/\ device.lensSeparationDistance*0.5f)/device.hScreenSize;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01240\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ config.leftLensCenter[0]\ =\ 0.25f\ +\ lensShift;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01241\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ config.leftLensCenter[1]\ =\ 0.5f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01242\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ config.rightLensCenter[0]\ =\ 0.75f\ -\/\ lensShift;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01243\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ config.rightLensCenter[1]\ =\ 0.5f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01244\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ config.leftScreenCenter[0]\ =\ 0.25f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01245\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ config.leftScreenCenter[1]\ =\ 0.5f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01246\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ config.rightScreenCenter[0]\ =\ 0.75f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01247\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ config.rightScreenCenter[1]\ =\ 0.5f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01248\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01249\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Compute\ distortion\ scale\ parameters}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01250\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ NOTE:\ To\ get\ lens\ max\ radius,\ lensShift\ must\ be\ normalized\ to\ [-\/1..1]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01251\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ lensRadius\ =\ fabsf(-\/1.0f\ -\/\ 4.0f*lensShift);}
\DoxyCodeLine{01252\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ lensRadiusSq\ =\ lensRadius*lensRadius;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01253\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ distortionScale\ =\ device.lensDistortionValues[0]\ +}
\DoxyCodeLine{01254\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ device.lensDistortionValues[1]*lensRadiusSq\ +}
\DoxyCodeLine{01255\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ device.lensDistortionValues[2]*lensRadiusSq*lensRadiusSq\ +}
\DoxyCodeLine{01256\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ device.lensDistortionValues[3]*lensRadiusSq*lensRadiusSq*lensRadiusSq;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01257\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01258\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ normScreenWidth\ =\ 0.5f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01259\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ normScreenHeight\ =\ 1.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01260\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ config.scaleIn[0]\ =\ 2.0f/normScreenWidth;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01261\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ config.scaleIn[1]\ =\ 2.0f/normScreenHeight/aspect;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01262\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ config.scale[0]\ =\ normScreenWidth*0.5f/distortionScale;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01263\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ config.scale[1]\ =\ normScreenHeight*0.5f*aspect/distortionScale;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01264\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01265\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Fovy\ is\ normally\ computed\ with:\ 2*atan2f(device.vScreenSize,\ 2*device.eyeToScreenDistance)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01266\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ ...but\ with\ lens\ distortion\ it\ is\ increased\ (see\ Oculus\ SDK\ Documentation)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01267\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ fovy\ =\ 2.0f*atan2f(device.vScreenSize*0.5f*distortionScale,\ device.eyeToScreenDistance);\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Really\ need\ distortionScale?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01268\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ float\ fovy\ =\ 2.0f*(float)atan2f(device.vScreenSize*0.5f,\ device.eyeToScreenDistance);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01269\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01270\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Compute\ camera\ projection\ matrices}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01271\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ projOffset\ =\ 4.0f*lensShift;\ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Scaled\ to\ projection\ space\ coordinates\ [-\/1..1]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01272\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{structMatrix}{Matrix}}\ proj\ =\ MatrixPerspective(fovy,\ aspect,\ rlGetCullDistanceNear(),\ rlGetCullDistanceFar());}
\DoxyCodeLine{01273\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01274\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ config.projection[0]\ =\ MatrixMultiply(proj,\ MatrixTranslate(projOffset,\ 0.0f,\ 0.0f));}
\DoxyCodeLine{01275\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ config.projection[1]\ =\ MatrixMultiply(proj,\ MatrixTranslate(-\/projOffset,\ 0.0f,\ 0.0f));}
\DoxyCodeLine{01276\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01277\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Compute\ camera\ transformation\ matrices}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01278\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ NOTE:\ Camera\ movement\ might\ seem\ more\ natural\ if\ we\ model\ the\ head}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01279\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Our\ axis\ of\ rotation\ is\ the\ base\ of\ our\ head,\ so\ we\ might\ want\ to\ add}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01280\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ some\ y\ (base\ of\ head\ to\ eye\ level)\ and\ -\/z\ (center\ of\ head\ to\ eye\ protrusion)\ to\ the\ camera\ positions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01281\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ config.viewOffset[0]\ =\ MatrixTranslate(device.interpupillaryDistance*0.5f,\ 0.075f,\ 0.045f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{01282\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ config.viewOffset[1]\ =\ MatrixTranslate(-\/device.interpupillaryDistance*0.5f,\ 0.075f,\ 0.045f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{01283\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01284\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Compute\ eyes\ Viewports}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01533\ \ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{structVector3}{Vector3}}\ nearPoint\ =\ Vector3Unproject((\mbox{\hyperlink{structVector3}{Vector3}})\{\ deviceCoords.x,\ deviceCoords.y,\ 0.0f\ \},\ matProj,\ matView);}

\DoxyCodeLine{01538\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ compared\ to\ perspective\ doesn't\ have\ a\ convergence\ point,}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01562\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Get\ camera\ 2d\ transform\ matrix}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01563\ \mbox{\hyperlink{structMatrix}{Matrix}}\ GetCameraMatrix2D(\mbox{\hyperlink{structCamera2D}{Camera2D}}\ camera)}
\DoxyCodeLine{01564\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{01565\ \ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{structMatrix}{Matrix}}\ matTransform\ =\ \{\ 0\ \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{01566\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ camera\ in\ world-\/space\ is\ set\ by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01567\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ 1.\ Move\ it\ to\ target}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01568\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ 2.\ Rotate\ by\ -\/rotation\ and\ scale\ by\ (1/zoom)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01569\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ When\ setting\ higher\ scale,\ it's\ more\ intuitive\ for\ the\ world\ to\ become\ bigger\ (=\ camera\ become\ smaller),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01570\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ not\ for\ the\ camera\ getting\ bigger,\ hence\ the\ invert.\ Same\ deal\ with\ rotation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01571\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ 3.\ Move\ it\ by\ (-\/offset);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01572\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ Offset\ defines\ target\ transform\ relative\ to\ screen,\ but\ since\ we're\ effectively\ "{}moving"{}\ screen\ (camera)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01573\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ we\ need\ to\ do\ it\ into\ opposite\ direction\ (inverse\ transform)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01574\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01575\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Having\ camera\ transform\ in\ world-\/space,\ inverse\ of\ it\ gives\ the\ modelview\ transform}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01576\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Since\ (A*B*C)'\ =\ C'*B'*A',\ the\ modelview\ is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01577\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ 1.\ Move\ to\ offset}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01578\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ 2.\ Rotate\ and\ Scale}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01579\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ 3.\ Move\ by\ -\/target}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01580\ \ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{structMatrix}{Matrix}}\ matOrigin\ =\ MatrixTranslate(-\/camera.target.x,\ -\/camera.target.y,\ 0.0f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{01581\ \ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{structMatrix}{Matrix}}\ matRotation\ =\ MatrixRotate((\mbox{\hyperlink{structVector3}{Vector3}})\{\ 0.0f,\ 0.0f,\ 1.0f\ \},\ camera.rotation*DEG2RAD);}
\DoxyCodeLine{01582\ \ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{structMatrix}{Matrix}}\ matScale\ =\ MatrixScale(camera.zoom,\ camera.zoom,\ 1.0f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{01583\ \ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{structMatrix}{Matrix}}\ matTranslation\ =\ MatrixTranslate(camera.offset.x,\ camera.offset.y,\ 0.0f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{01584\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01585\ \ \ \ \ matTransform\ =\ MatrixMultiply(MatrixMultiply(matOrigin,\ MatrixMultiply(matScale,\ matRotation)),\ matTranslation);}
\DoxyCodeLine{01586\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01587\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return}\ matTransform;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01588\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01589\ }
